***blozen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blozen.html>blozen</a> (15449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blosen</i>, further etymology unclear, but ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blus-</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">blosen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">bloazje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Swedish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Swedish">Old Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmq-osw">blusa</i>, and with <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">blöschen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">blȳsian</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blozen.html>blozen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blush, to flush</li></ol>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">blue</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bell</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bluebell.html>bluebell</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bluebells.html>bluebells</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Various flowering plants with blue, usually pendulous, flowers.

<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_bluebell" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish bluebell">Spanish <a href = vnd.unilang:bluebell.html>bluebell</a></a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Hyacinthoides_hispanica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Hyacinthoides hispanica"><i>Hyacinthoides hispanica</i></a></span>)</li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_bluebell" class="extiw" title="w:Italian bluebell">Italian <a href = vnd.unilang:bluebell.html>bluebell</a></a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Hyacinthoides_italica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Hyacinthoides italica"><i>Hyacinthoides italica</i></a></span>)</li></ol></li>
<li>In other genera
<ol><li>genus <i>Muscari</i>, the grape hyacinth)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virginia_bluebell" class="extiw" title="w:Virginia bluebell">Virginia <a href = vnd.unilang:bluebell.html>bluebell</a></a> (<i>Mertensia virginica</i>)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> bluff (10869)</h1><br></body> 
***bluffen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bluffen.html>bluffen</a> (12792)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bluffen.html>bluffen</a></i>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">verblüffen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stump, perplex</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bluff</i>, which may be borrowed from Dutch. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boa.html>boa</a> (47738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:boa.html>boa</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:boa.html>boa</a></i>. The use for scarf derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:boa.html>boa</a></i>.

<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boa.html>boa</a></span>, snake of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:boa.html>Boa</a></i></li>

***bob.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bob.html>bob</a> (1103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewust.html>bewust</a> onbeschonken <a href = vnd.unilang:bestuurder.html>bestuurder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deliberately unintoxicated driver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bobcat.html>bobcat</a> (84664)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bob.html>bob</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">short hair; with reference to its tail</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cat</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bobcat.html>bobcat</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bobcats.html>bobcats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A North American wild cat, <i>Lynx <a href = vnd.unilang:rufus.html>rufus</a></i>, having tufted ears and a short tail.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i>Lynx <a href = vnd.unilang:rufus.html>rufus</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">red lynx</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Genericization of the trademark <a href = vnd.unilang:bobcat.html>Bobcat</a>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bobcat.html>bobcat</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bobcats.html>bobcats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a multi-purpose construction vehicle, akin to a <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> version of a front-end loader or a backhoe (backhoe loader), with a one-man caged control cabin</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bodemprijs.html>bodemprijs</a> (84660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bodem.html>bodem</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bottom, lowest point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prijs.html>prijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">price</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bodyguard.html>bodyguard</a> (13315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">body</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">guard</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bodyguard.html>bodyguard</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bodyguards.html>bodyguards</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person or group of persons, often armed, responsible for protecting an individual.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bodyguard.html>bodyguard</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bodyguards.html>bodyguards</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bodyguarding</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bodyguarded</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To act as <a href = vnd.unilang:bodyguard.html>bodyguard</a> for (someone); <i>figuratively</i>, to protect.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:boedel.html>boedel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*buothal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bōþl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bōþlą</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:boef.html>boef</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boeve</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bouve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*buovo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bōbô</i>, a reduplicated form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bō-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">father, brother, male relative</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></i>, Pennsylvania Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="pdt"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>Bub</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bube</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">bófi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rogue, knave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related also to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:babe.html>babe</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">boy</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boeien.html>boeien</a> (4285)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boeyen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boei.html>boei</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tie down, tie up, bind, shackle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to captivate, fascinate, interest

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boeit.html>boeit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:denkt.html>denkt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What you think doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>interest</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> (582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boec</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">buok</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bōks</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Book</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Buch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">book</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">bog</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boekanier.html>boekanier</a> (95027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">boucanier</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boekanier.html>boekanier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boekaniers.html>boekaniers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:buccaneer.html>buccaneer</a>, pirate; originally especially in reference to French <a href = vnd.unilang:pirates.html>pirates</a> and privateers operating in the Caribbean

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boel.html>boel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boel.html>boelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeltje.html>boeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a lot, bunch
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boel.html>boel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a>!</i>

<li>mess, disorderly heap</li>
<li>quarrel
<dl><dd><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Brabantian</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wee.html>wee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boel.html>boel</a></b> in da rucht cafe!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>trouble</b> again in that infamous <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>!</span></dd></dl></div>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boele</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male relative</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, further etymology unknown. May belong to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bō-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">father, brother, close male relation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">lover</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">adulterer</span>, someone who commits adultery</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:boenen.html>boenen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bōnon</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bōnen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bōnōną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bōnijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to polish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***boer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a> (3550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bure</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*būr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*būraz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dweller, inhabitant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus originally the same as modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buur.html>buur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">neighbour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that of many eastern dialects including <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limburgish" class="extiw" title="w:Limburgish">Limburgish</a></span>, where Germanic <i>-ū-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> retained as a back vowel. In early modern Dutch these two dialectal forms <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> adopted as semantically distinguished <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">būr</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġebūr</i> (whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bower.html>bower</a></i>) and Old High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">būr</i> (whence German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bauer</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boertje.html>boertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerin.html>boerin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(male) farmer, peasant
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bouwman</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym"><span class="defdate">Hyponyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:landbouwer.html>landbouwer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">teler</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuinder.html>tuinder</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veehouder.html>veehouder</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in compounds</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> merchant (and sometimes producer) of a certain product group, mainly foods, often named after it, e.g. <a href = vnd.unilang:melkboer.html>melkboer</a> 'milkman', <a href = vnd.unilang:groenteboer.html>groenteboer</a> '(male) greengrocer'</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:boor.html>boor</a>, yokel, ruffian</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> (playing card)</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally onomatopoetic, as <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">burp</i>. The perception of farmers (etymology 1) as being mannerless people <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> probably played a secondary role, too. The same in German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bäuerchen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boertje.html>boertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A belch, a burp.</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to farm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">place associated with an activity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the interfixed <i>-d-</i> originally being a dialectal element.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a> (3463)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">farmer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to farm, practice agriculture</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do (well, badly...) in some business</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to burp, to belch</li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">farmer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerenjongen.html>boerenjongen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerenjongens.html>boerenjongens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerenjongetje.html>boerenjongetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">common</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">farmboy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">country-boy</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Bart <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echte.html>echte</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boerenjongen.html>boerenjongen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> inwijkeling <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Bart <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a real <b>farmboy</b>, no immigrant from the city.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>a farmer's boy, i.e. son</li>
<li>an alcoholic beverage with <a href = vnd.unilang:brandy.html>brandy</a> and raisins</li>
<li>raisin drenched in <a href = vnd.unilang:brandy.html>brandy</a></li></ol>
